***закрепить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрепить.html>закрепи́ть</a> (6632)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крепить.html>крепи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрепить.html>закрепи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakrepítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закреплять.html>закрепля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fasten, to secure, to fix, to attach, to mount, to anchor</li>
<li>to consolidate, to strengthen</li>
<li>to allot</li></ol>

***закрепляться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрепляться.html>закрепля́ться</a> (25660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закреплять.html>закрепля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakrepljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрепляться.html>закрепля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakrepljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрепиться.html>закрепи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to consolidate one's grip <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрепляться.html>закрепля́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:позиция.html>пози́ции</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrepljátʹsja</b> na pozícii</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to consolidate a position</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закреплять.html>закрепля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakrepljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kričátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***закружить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закружить.html>закружи́ть</a> (19566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружить.html>кружи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kružítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закружить.html>закружи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakružítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружить.html>кружи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to begin to turn/whirl, to send whirling</li>
<li>to make dizzy, to sweep off one's feet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закружить.html>закружи́ть</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:танец.html>та́нце</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakružítʹ</b> kovó-libo v tánce</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make someone's head turn with dancing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"> 
</th>

***закружиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закружиться.html>закружи́ться</a> (8978)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закружить.html>закружи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakružítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закружиться.html>закружи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakružítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кружиться.html>кружи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to begin to whirl/spin, to begin to go round
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:закружиться.html>закружи́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u menjá <b>zakružílasʹ</b> golová</i> ― <span class="e-translation">my head began to swim</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be run off one's feet, to be in a whirl
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закружиться.html>закружи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йством</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakružítʹsja</b> s xozjájstvom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">be run off one's feet with (the) housework [with domestic chores]</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***закрутить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a> (9702)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakrutítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутить.html>крути́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to twirl, to twist, to wind around
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спи́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrutítʹ</b> komú-libo rúki za spínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to twist someone's arms behind his back</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вожжа.html>во́жжи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrutítʹ</b> vóžži na rúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wind the reins round one's hands</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ус.html>усы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrutítʹ</b> usý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn up the ends of one's moustache; twirl/twiddle/twist one's moustache</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пыль.html>пыль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véter <b>zakrutíl</b> pylʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wind is stirring up the dust</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:роман.html>рома́н</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrutítʹ</b> román (s)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have/start an affair (with)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(tap etc)</i> to turn off, <i>(nut etc)</i> to turn tight, to tighten <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гайка.html>га́йки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zakrutítʹ gájki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tighten the screws <i>(on someone)</i></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрутиться.html>закрути́ться</a> (15205)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakrutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутиться.html>закрути́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakrutítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">закру́чиваться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to twist, to become twisted</li>
<li>to become screwed up</li>
<li>to begin to turn</li>
<li>to be tied up with one's affairs, to be bound up in one's affairs</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakrutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***закручивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a> (23871)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakrutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakrúčivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутить.html>закрути́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to twirl, to twist, to wind round
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спи́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrúčivatʹ</b> komú-libo rúki za spínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to twist someone's arms behind his back</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вожжа.html>во́жжи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>ру́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrúčivatʹ</b> vóžži na rúki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wind the reins round one's hands</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ус.html>усы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakrúčivatʹ</b> usý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to turn up the ends of one's moustache; twirl/twiddle/twist one's moustache</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(tap etc)</i> to turn off, <i>(nut etc)</i> to turn tight, to tighten <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закручивать.html>закру́чивать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гайка.html>га́йки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zakrúčivatʹ gájki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to tighten the screws <i>(on someone)</i></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">закру́чиваться</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zakrúčivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрутиться.html>закрути́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zakrutítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрывать.html>закрыва́ть</a> (2287)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрыть.html>закры́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakrýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрывать.html>закрыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрыть.html>закры́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cover</li>
<li>to hide</li>
<li>to close, to shut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрывать.html>закрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крышка.html>кры́шку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakryvátʹ</b> krýšku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to <b>close</b> the lid</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закрыть.html>закры́ть</a> (1134)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крыть.html>крыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">krytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрыть.html>закры́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakrýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закрывать.html>закрыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cover, to hide</li>
<li>to close, to shut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:закрыть.html>закры́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>zakrýl</b> dverʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>closed</b> the door.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
